    SELECT TOP(2) [ı].[InvoiceId], [ı].[CompanyId], [ı].[DueDate], [ı].[ExcludingVat], [ı].[InvoiceNu], [ı].[InvoiceType], [ı].[IsComplete], [ı].[Name], [ı].[StatusCode], [ı].[Total], [ı].[TotalVat], [ı].[UserId]
